Medium shot. We see a police jeep driving up a rough looking road in the middle of the night with the headlights and the blue and reds flashing on top glowing through the darkness. ?Box?This is Sheriff Jones, I’m just arriving at the camp site. Is there any word on the paramedic? ?2. Medium shot. The jeep is driving up towards the campsite with the headlights showing off the damaged SUV and the burnt out wreck that crashed into it.?Radio?Copy that, they are on rout as we speak. ?3. Medium shot. Getting out of the jeep we see the sheriff getting out with a very confused look on his face. His name is Jones. ?Jones (confused)?What the hell happened here??4. Medium shot. Leaning in to the car Jones is reaching for a large bulky flash on the passenger’s seat.?5. Medium shot. Jones is now looking around with his large flashlight in his left hand and his right resting on his gun in its holster. ?Jones (yelling)?Police! Anybody here???Page 2 (of 6)?1. Large shot. Jones has stopped in horror as he finds the bloody and shredded tent in the wide beams of his torch as he feels to remove the gun from its holster.?Jones (horrified)?Oh Jesus! ?2. Medium shot. Jones is now racing back to his jeep with a fast sprint and a look of disbelief on his face and placing his gun back in the holster. ?3. Medium shot. We see Jones leaning in grabbing the radio from next to the steering wheel still holding on to the torch. ?4. Medium shot. As Jones is leaning into his car to use the radio we see Kelly from behind slowly walking towards him from the darkness, Jones having no idea. ?Jones (shock)?Control, you need to cancel that ambulance and get state patrol out here, we got a crime scene…??Page 3 (of 6)?1. Large shot. Suddenly Jones is being pulled from the car from behind as we are in the car looking at his surprised face. ?Jones (surprised)?What the hell!??2. Medium shot. We see Jones with the torch between him and the zombie Kelly who has half of the flesh on her face ripped and chewed away preventing her from biting him and the light shining up under her head and lighting her face like telling a ghost story around a camp fire. ?Jones (scared)?Oh Jesus lady what’s wrong with you!??3. Medium shot. Jones manages to force her back and on to the ground with great force while reaching for his gun. ?Jones (scared)?Get off me lady!!!?4. Medium shot. Kelly is climbing back up again to give another attack as Jones is stood there with both arms stretched out holding the torch and the gun towards her with the look of panic on his face.?Jones (scared)?Just stay back for Christ sake, I mean it!?5. Medium shot. As Kelly leaps up towards Jones he shoots her square in the head with the bullet passing straight through with a bloody mess. ??Page 4 (of 6)?1. Medium shot. Suddenly the zombie Jim comes out of the darkness and is grabbing hold of Jones’s left arm and the torch as he has no time to react.?Jones (scared)?Christ another one!!!?2. Close up shot. Jim is now biting into his hand drawing blood as Jones drops the torch to the ground. ?Jones (screaming)?AARRRG!!!!?3. Medium shot. Jones is now shooting Jim in the head to get him off his hand with another spray of blood as the bullet passes through the brain. ?Jones (screaming)?GET OFF ME!!!?4. Medium shot. Jones is now inspecting his hand to see a large chunk missing and his little finger barely staying on.?Jones (in pain)?Oh fuck!!!?5. Medium shot. He is now climbing back into his jeep to in great pain to get out of the area as fast as possible, both the bodies of the dead zombies still on the ground. ??Page 5 (of 6)?1. Medium shot. We are now looking at an ambulance speeding up an empty highway through the night with all its lights on. ?Box?I think the exit is up ahead.?2. Medium shot. Looking inside to front of the ambulance through the front windshield we see a male paramedic call Boon and his female colleague Wendy as they are keeping an eye out.?Wendy (calm)?You sure it’s around here??Boon (calm)?Yeah my dad used to bring me here as a kid.?3. Medium shot. Both suddenly have shocked looks on their faces as they can see something off panel. ?Boon (shocked)?Christ almighty!!!?4. Large shot. The ambulance is pulling up the crashed police jeep that still has its own lights flashing. It has collided with a street sign causing damage to the front. ??Page 6 (of 6)?1. Large shot. Both paramedics are racing out of the front towards the crashed jeep carrying first aid kits with them. ?Wendy (confused)?This the right call? ?2. Medium shot. Boon is now in the driver’s door inspecting the unconscious but alive Jones with his bite wound on the hand visible.?Boon (rushed)?Car crash and bite mark, seems right to me. Let’s get him on the move and call in for state patrol and rescue to commence a search though just to be sure. ?3. Medium shot. Both paramedics are wheeling the unconscious Sheriff to the back of the ambulance, Wendy climbing into the back as she pulls. ?Wendy (reassuring)?Don’t worry Sheriff, we will have you in the hospital in twenty minutes. Just hang in there, ok??4. Medium shot. Boon is closing the back of the ambulance sealing Wendy in with Jones and does it in a rush.?Boon (rushed)?Ok let’s get going!?Text?To be
